Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your cure is not beneficial, then you must make four cauterizations around the wound, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the heart, two behind the back on the spine, and one at the anus.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterization be close to the specific heart beat.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cauterization open for a long time to allow pus to drain, do not neglect the care of the patient after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will happen more quickly, and the two sides will be aligned with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cauterization for the abdomen should be like the claw that we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and make it olive-shaped, according to what is mentioned above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of stones
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in the hydroptic patient and filled with yellow pus, you should cauterize the back between the little finger and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and hold your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not press too deeply, so as to close the citrus-colored eyes, and perform the cauterization according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After that, make two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the scalpel;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cautery be long, one of the sockets of the knee in front and the other behind, on the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries overlong without dressing, so that they heal in place.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the dressing of the other wounds that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the joint
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When abdominal distension arises from cold and moisture, the retention and digestion of virtues in the stomach and intestines is weakened, and it cannot be cured by any means.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great pain, so make a strong cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken before, or a cautery for the circulatory system.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and I cauterize around the anus gently with a delicate cautery, and I cauterize the glands.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, apply a cautery to the wrist, one cautery on each side, and two small cauteries on the stomach to remove the excessive, for the cure is beneficial when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	On the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are at the base or in greater numbers, and they have been old, consisting of corrupted cold and moist humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and do not benefit, then make cauterization.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On the spine of the back, those who are entirely devoid of strength should slowly and gradually stretch, and by cauterizing the roots of the nerves, they should ease the pain in two ways.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is chilled, and the meat does not cook, and swelling appears on the face, then great cauterization should be applied to the stomach, as mentioned before, and another on the liver, and another across every part of the cauterization with a clamp.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the open cauterization for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, reset the joint as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	from the fleshiness called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you are completely healed, if you feel the fire of cautery as sharp as a razor, and then apply it thoroughly over that entire area.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let it stay until the cautery reaches the vein, from which comes the blood.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much tissue, cauterize each as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the beneficial treatment of wounds while they are clean;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a hot cautery on the raw flesh, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	From the badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, as we shall relate in its place, a disease arises that can only be healed by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a vein becomes fistulated, inflamed, filled with putridity and corrupt moisture, you must try all sorts of subtle treatments, and be sure to understand the full effect of each one.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery to a sharp point, insert it into the fistula according to the amount that has entered, and repeat the cauterization until the dead or corrupted flesh is completely burned, once, or twice, or three times, depending on the amount required.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is sensitive, and great vessels.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula is in the wall of the bladder and the intestine, be careful of these vessels, and do not make any fire except on fatty flesh, and think that it is not painful.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After healing the limb as long as it is healthy, and if its joints are flexible, and the bones are slowly pulled out, then you know that the joint is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the bones are not slowly pulled out, know that the joint is damaged and corrupted deep within the bone.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus, as one of these would tell us about their joint.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When the pain of a fracture comes with heavy bleeding and cannot be managed by women, then you must perform cauterization on the wound on both sides using the cautery iron we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and so we cauterize it in the middle, if there are three cauterizations in a row, and they will provide greater aid.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then it should be cauterized in the upper part, just below where the urethra begins, with both hands, on the right and left sides, making each cauterization as long as our thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and cauterize it further down the back if necessary.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cautery be performed according to the shape mentioned above.
de la marris	From the sea
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the soil is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends are delayed.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they cause great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to make three cauterizations around the wound, as we have said about the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and so the cautery of the bone, as we have said.
de la hainche	de la hainche" translates to "of the neck
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When sticky moisture descends into the chest cavity and for this reason it cannot move from its place, and the signs are that the affected limb is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found that the internal organs move strangely, so it is necessary to cauterize the patient over the chest cavity with a cautery in the shape of a circle, and mark around the joint as it moves, so that the chest remains within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if it is the cautery like those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present to you, then make three cauterizations from the large olive, and let these cauterizations be as good as all the others.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as long as it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain arises in the chest due to cold and moisture, and the patient is afflicted with this condition for a long time, treatment as described in the previous section may not be effective, and the disease becomes chronic.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	So it is necessary for you to purge the patient of bad humours from foul pills, or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterwards, perform cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of cautery is according to two manners:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	this involves the use of burning medicines and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many manners, of which some are as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the wound of the neck with three cautery triangles, cauterizing them according to this form, making them deep and wide, and leaving enough space between each cautery for the thickness of two fingers, and they should be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	one should never cauterize in the middle of the neck, which is why there are three according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	and if you see that cauterization with the circular cautery we have mentioned in the dislocation of the neck is not effective.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circles contain all the pain, and every part of the heart is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used for sciatica, when the pain is in the hip and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	and if it extends to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations below where the patient feels the pain, and one cauterization above the ankle on the left side slightly.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let it be a knife cauterization, and burn the thickness of the heart.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels the pain extending to both feet or near the anus, cauterize that area where it hurts three times or four with a point cauterization.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it happens more, he must do so;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is in the knee towards the thigh, he should perform cautery with a cutting or circular instrument, and be careful in all his cauterizations that he does not leave the cautery for too long, lest he burns the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause the patient greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I myself have seen many who have made cuts on the ankle of the foot and left them until the leg was completely swollen, and also the ankle, making it pierced and corrupted all over the ankle.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal solution, he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, apply cautery to one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones say about the cautery of the hainche (knee), which is the way, make the iron as thick as a new dime or slightly thinner, and twist it between them or intertwine them one after the other with a distance equal to the size of a thumb's nail.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and intertwine them over both parts, and make them as if they were new, and have a well-made iron of each.
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and heat it until it is completely red and exudes pus, then place it on the diseased haunch of the animal, and turn to the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and apply the cautery once the cauterization is complete, and leave it for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply an ointment of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of the ointment as long as it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albuscasim says that we should use this cautery little because of the fear of its regard, and see little of those who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and nevertheless, these are good cauteries, which the patient can endure, and the place where it is performed.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	He uses the cautery of hot medicine, so make you an instrument to intertwine with which you lower the edge of the door, and it is of iron or steel on a long wall, and at its highest point there are two, and between each there is the quantity of thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they should be open above and below, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After that, place the board of the spine on the patient lying on their side, and quickly place your hand above the board of the spine.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After pouring between the two circles of hot awes (coals) that have been heated over fire, leave them for an hour while the patient endures the heat and burn.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	Because it has the same effect as fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the blisters have passed, take your hand with the instrument and lift the strip of soft awes, leaving it for three days, and apply butter until the blackening from the burn disappears;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it for three more days until the putrefaction subsides;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this should be the last aid after the treatment of wounds as long as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or the leg, use the instrument that suits according to what you have done in increasing the joint.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of hot air, which I have written about in treating rectal medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, both in equal amounts, grind them together, and put them into a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or if he has a small opening, defuse it so that the point of a needle can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place over it some well-beaten lead or other, and lay chalk and alum gently on top, as much as there are two layers of powder when you hold it in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until all the water and mud have dried, then take all that water and pour it on chalk and alum as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And thus, it will be most effective and beneficial in many cases of medical emergencies and other cauterization of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the same action as fire, and if used with other medicines to cauterize the pain such as fennel, anise, and calamus mixed with soap, all these things combined.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment by which one noble was cured of the pain in his back and sciatic nerve, and he recovered completely, and they did not use any other treatment, and he remained well once this cure was performed, and he bathed as he teaches below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And prepare it in this manner: you press the fresh and dry verdigris and grind it finely with a little fat, then apply it to the pain, on the hip and thigh and leg, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours, or until the patient no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter a bath or water as long as the body is slightly warmed, and make him lie down, and the pain will disappear completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery with such medicines unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's dung, it provides great relief.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery should be performed in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lint and grease it with old oil, and apply it to the groove that is between the big toe and the one called the 'fossa'.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dried goat's dung, ignite it with fire until it becomes charcoal, and place it on the cloth, leaving it until it is stained.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and repeat this process, ceasing only when you believe through sense that the pain has ceased, reaching up to the waist.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and these kinds of cautery are called "fire cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the painful back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain arises in the back, whether from pulling or compression or excessive blood evacuation or some similar matter that appears expanded and cold, none of these appearances warrant cauterization, except for that which comes from the infusion of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after the patient is freed of foul pills or other similar substances, that one makes three incisions on the back, where the pain resides, with each line marked with a sign, and in each line performs five cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and these cauterizations are performed according to the cautery called "point".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauterizations at the "key hole" according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often afflicts young children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a tight and painful throat when they swallow, and they feel weak.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you will feel in the last, most severe pain in the back and, appearing differently, it comes upon the other pains.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this, and you observe its cure, cauterize it with fire according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cauterization may heal each part of the wound equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see that the cauterization around the wound pierces with the cautery two or three lines, and the points are close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure, hold the limb until it is healthy according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cautery to any numb areas that are affected by nerve damage.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain in the joints is caused by moisture that spreads to each limb of the body, and when a sharp pain occurs, they call it "podagra" properly; and when it is due to a cold cause and cannot be cured by medicine, it is treated with cautery in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the mouth of cautery around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to pin the sole of the foot, make a cautery in the shape of a "dot".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, and this often happens, then make cautery on each knee with three or four cauterizations from each part, keeping the entire cautery olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, then do so, but don't hold your hand too tightly until the thickness of the heart is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and to the back, he should apply the cautery as we have said in his chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are intense, make points around the wound with two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is no pain remaining, make points on each joint and on the skin of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come up to the neck or shoulders, cauterize each part and apply a good compress to the patient and take medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you govern it well and drain the moisture, it will be healed by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the rupture of the sinew.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When the wound becomes infected, and the boils descend to the joints, which is new, it is necessary that when you see him being cured, he does not move too much on that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things which leave the stomach, so that the intestines descend from his stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after making him lie on his back between your hands, and commanding him to keep his breath until the boils are healed, arrange them in order at your will, and sign with your finger from inside the fracture on the arm bone, and make a mark that resembles half a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery instrument with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and it sheds scales.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bones to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the healer places his hand upon it, so that they do not return backwards;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open well the thighs of the patient, and place beneath him cushions and supports on the thighs, and others on the pelvis that hold his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery instrument upon the sign with your entire hand, and hold it straight and firm until you reach the bone, and if you do not touch it the first time, repeat it again until you do, reaching as close to the bone as possible.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard carefully so that the boil does not burst when you perform the cauterization.
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient does not die or suffer other evils.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is useless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to their size, and also for adults, as great according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, treat the wound with butter until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After treating other wounds as long as they are healthy, and the patient lies on their back for forty days until the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that these movements be held for a long time, so that the boils do not appear when he moves to his room.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to stand up, a well-made bandage is applied to him and left for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and have good rest, that he works little and guards himself from too much drinking and eating, and from excessive noise.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he gives this instruction, he heals them completely.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will now describe the treatment for cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures occur in other organs and are known not to heal, you will see that they do not grow back. Therefore, apply fire cautery according to its quantity, burning the third part of the wound.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and no of the ancients said that it must be cauterized with fire at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first sign the skin with a sharp instrument and make a line across the width above the dislocation, and another one further away, and hold your hand firmly over the entire cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the initial cauterization is lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any member, either from weakness or an injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and the medicine provides no relief, then it is necessary to cauterize the affected area with a instrument called "poins," and the cauterization should be done according to the length of the member, its smallness or largeness, its strength or weakness, its position, and the nature of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If he is sane after the first cautery, that's good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this does not help, begin another cautery on that part, as it is customary for the limb to move on its own; therefore, you should perform cauteries until the patient is sane.
de meselerie	It seems like there might have been a slight error or missing
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	These diseases are never helped by a single cautery, especially the illness that arises from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	As you cauterize, be mindful if the disease is in its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the previous section, without delay or movement, but if you doubt that the corruption might spread throughout the patient, then perform cautery on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I cut off the new hair at the root, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the beard.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and then on both horns, and behind on the scalp.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I hold the patient's hand so that the fire cautery comes close to the bone, and until the skin is broken out so that the vapors of the thick humors can come out.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize the mouse according to what it needs.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the disorder is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is evident that you need to apply these cauterizations that we have mentioned above: first, cauterize the new growths, second, cauterize on the spine of the nape, third, cauterize on the spine of the back, fourth, strongly on the hip joint and another delicate one, fifth, on both shoulders.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and second, on the sides, and second, on the tendons of the foot, and first, on each joint of the hands and feet, and in the palm pits.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and guard the nerves that are above the deepest pressure, so as not to burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never perform cautery on the bones of the fingers or other bones, such as those of the stomach or liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cautery is done, the greater the benefit it brings, and the more it helps.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient feels no pain from cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be great or small according to the members and joints, as you will find in the manner of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply a poultice of meal with honey and other remedies until it is cleansed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling appears in any member and is treated with medicines, oils, and bandages, but it does not heal, then one should perform cautery on the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and the cautery should be slightly inserted into the heart's space.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure the wounds as long as they are healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never should cautery be performed on the hand, foot, or back, at the end of the nerve that numbs the member, and thus is removed the swelling.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and nevertheless, no one should intervene unless they know the parts and the passages of the moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	Of alba (or white)
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is raging, and the medical art avails nothing, then cauterize with a hot iron a little bit, according to the extent of the pain, until the white (flesh) is removed, and it changes color.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then apply a remedy of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and collicul (a type of herb) and alder bark, each in its own portion.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and it should be mixed with all together, tied with a cloth, and moved towards the light as long as it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of the ulcer (chancre) by cauterization.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a ulcer (chancre) appears in its initial stages, and you wish to stop its progression, cauterize it with an iron that forms a circle around the entire ulcer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Nevertheless, the wise say that one should also perform cautery in the middle of a ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and yet, this does not seem good to me, as I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it succeed before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and there is a more correct practice that it should be cauterized around, in the cautery called "circle", as we have said in many cauterization methods.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	from the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati," and it takes time to die, either because of the excess it produces or due to the great pain of the illness when the patient is old (that is, too much), and there is little blood, or because of the time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hasten to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around with small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterward leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierce through entirely with the cautery, the heat of which is as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the midst of this ill-named 'adubelati' (disease) while the cautery has pierced through, making it like the cautery so that the patient feels no further pain in such a way that the course of the rotting is halted.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease is called "corrodens," which is nothing other than a weakening of the limbs, as it affects the members just as fire does dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in the body that can be treated with fire cautery, then heat the cautery tools slightly and thoroughly, according to what is suitable for the part or the illness.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After cauterizing all parts as long as you can see all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, ensure that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and place on the joints cauterized, suffering from burning with oil until all the scorches from the fire are healed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of wounds that cause pain.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy hair does not grow, it is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if this is not the case, then repeat the cautery on what remains of the corrupted part.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this treatment is sometimes cured with a hot medicinal drink instead of fire cautery.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but fire cautery is still of greater help, and I have already described the treatment with hot medicinal drinks in detail.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	from the pieces which come as fragments
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that pieces due to deficiencies arise a disease called "close" according to our intention, and it is a great wrong that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cautery for this disease is according to two manners.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, cautery with fire, and cautery with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	For fire cautery, you should be well-heated, just as if you were to sear with a brand, or a quill of hot iron, made to the appropriate size that it can pierce from all sides, and have sharp edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After heating everything hot on the nail, and turn your hand around the nail entirely until it reaches the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it thus for three days until it begins to fester;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of sage leaves ground with silk, and leave the poultice on all night; then the nail will break off and be pulled out from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure the wound with fresh, clean bandages until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are affected by fever and many times it occurs in hands and feet, then you should apply a hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a cane of iron or wood, or a feather from a dove, and place the nail and the glue, that is to say, the wart remover.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the cane around it so that it embraces everything, then add a little hot oil, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while rotating so that the edge of the cane reaches the root of the nail, and be able to find the hot water channel all the way to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and the patient endures a little the biting of hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it alone, and it will pull out at the root entirely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	First, make one after another, as you stretch all those that are in the body, then cure the wounds that cause pain.
li cure dou trembler	it cures the shaking of the body.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When anyone shivers from cold or trembles with quartan fever or another illness, it is necessary to make four cauterizations on the spine down the back, one cauterization between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and make one cauterization on the foot, and another cauterization on the stomach with an olive cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if he lets it tremble, and hastens the health of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	from pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Never is it apparent through external defects or pus-filled blisters that come from deeply corrupted, putrid matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	it is necessary at first, when they appear, to make cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery with fir wood, by which the point is seized in the fire, or with long roots of aristologe, or with a lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And under no circumstances should cautery be performed at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow worse in advance, but the excesses from which they come are broken, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times, serious complications arise from the blood of an artery that is cut during treatment, whether it be when opening a vein, incising an abscess, cauterizing a member, or similar procedures.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a great problem if it stinks.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	However, if this happens to anyone, you should hurry to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it very tightly until the pain is completely relieved from beneath your finger, and no more blood flows.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then place over the fire various small and large olive oil cauterizes until they are all red.

Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if a sudden spark flies when you cut your vein, and the cautery is extinguished, quickly take another from the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	and do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood stops flowing;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and ensure no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when there is no bleeding from the artery, it cannot be properly examined, especially when the artery is large, unless by one of the three methods we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by tightly binding threads, or by medications applied that have the power to stop blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and it becomes tightly bound and stretched.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers relief from a tight ligature by placing rags or burning items on it, or similar things, will not benefit unless he does so carefully.

et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move it, but apply cold moisture often as long as it is very cold until the flesh is frozen and swollen and numb.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and prepare, in advance, what is needed for cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	We begin the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all about the diseases that require fire cauterization or burning medicines, and we have explained their causes, tools, and forms of cauterization.

dou chief plein d’aigue	chief filled with water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes to children at birth, and when the head is squeezed too tightly during delivery.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and never comes from a known cause that we cannot explain.

et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this, I seem to think that it is better for me to abandon the work in part for some treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw children whose joints were filled with water, and the head grew larger each day that it could not hold itself up.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture was so severe that it became gangrene, and this moisture is gathered below the bone onto the syphac, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and if the dislocation is such that moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you must make a deep cut across the top with your knife.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as the moisture flows.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the form of the dislocation:

Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see the openings of the joints in each part widely open, and there is a sharp pain when you press it with your hand from inside, and it does not return to its place,
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary for you to cut into the head, make three cuts according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture completely.

puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then unbind it, and dress the wound with bandages and poultices, leaving the head equally restrained, and give the patient dry meat from a bag of moisture until the limb is comfortable and healed.

car aucune fois est elle devant;	because never is it before;
aucune fois derrier;	not at any time behind
aucune fois en destre;	never on the right side

de reume	Of the flame cautery, instruct the patient to
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone suffers from a disease called "cataract" in one or both eyes, and the illness is old, and medical treatment does not help, then the final remedy is the cautery with which they will cut the two arteries.

aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the limb with a rough cloth until the arteries open, then carefully extract the patient's collar with all the cloth.

de emigrainne	from migraine pain
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old migraine pain occurs, accompanied by catarrh due to moisture in the eyes and cheeks, and the persistent and similar symptoms of old age, it is treated with various medical cures, but often none of them help; then we must drain the arteries in the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of extracting them is that the patient pulls back the hairs from his temples, and finds the artery which opens in the temple, as it opens well with its pulse, and is little withdrawn outside, so that no one who is too quick can catch it.

por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for this is of greater help against moisture.

et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have this present, place ice on the wound until it is frozen, and raise the cold water as long as the wound continues, and strain it as appropriate.

Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	Because when the instruments are too tight, they hold the heat less.

des larmes	tears

de l’estoupement des oreilles	ear inflammation
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everyone who hears these words is one of the three things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or seeds, or animals, or stones from my mine or similar things as if to do:
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seeds, as in beans, peas, or other similar seeds:
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or things that flow away like water, smooth and clear, and similar objects.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When anything, whether it's a stone or another object that does not fit properly in the ear, causes pain or does not grow inside the ear, place the affected ear in the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see a stone, and it exudes any little drop of purple oil or sesame oil, then proceed with its removal.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and it causes sneezing due to condition, and it stops the nostrils when sneezing comes, and places around the ear pieces of cloth or wool.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and stretches the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times this treatment brings fever.
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, apply an extraction with subtle pincers, from which comes this form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	if it jumps out into the pincers, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if it does not, apply an extraction with a subtle, small-toothed forceps;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it still does not come out, make a thread and twist the head of the thread or punch a hole in the ear with great force, and plug up what is around the thread with soft wax so that the air cannot enter with the thread.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then take it off again as it was before, for many times it comes back just as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come back in this way, take plenty of care to prepare the instrument sharply for this purpose, and place a little cotton around it.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the pressure against the stone or anything else, and take it off again.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	and if none of these things that we have said work, then quickly split the ear so that the abscess hardens and stops moving.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the method of the incision is such that you first make the patient from the cephalica whole and extract the blood according to its virtue, then place the patient between your hands and bring the ear back upwards, and make a small incision at the base of the ear where the fat or tissue is attached;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and make the incision as wide as a moon, until you reach the stone, then remove it according to your ability, and suck it gently with your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains present and they swell, then administer an extraction.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot be extracted, then administer the mildest spatula according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make sure to perform a careful incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not attempt this if you believe the grains are moistened by earwax, as long as you have made many attempts.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it gently with pincers and suck, as we have said, so that the extraction is light.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the case where you extract something from the ear, it is necessary for the patient to use a strong sneeze immediately afterward and open the ear with cotton wool.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lay something on that same ear, whether there is moisture or not.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps through fire, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	if this does not help, take many needles according to the length of your finger, and heat them slightly over fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and then place the patient in a position where one of their feet is raised, and try to open the ear by inserting another needle from the other side, and use a third needle to press against the one inside the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and continue this process of needle against needle until the pain disappears completely, and thus it will disappear entirely.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you see, take a thin wire, and insert one end into the ear, and twist the other end gently over fire until the thinner wire is burned.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then make other adjustments of other joints until the pain completely disappears, as we said previously.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	When extracting a small creature, such as a bug or similar small object, treat it as we described in the previous section.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large and one can feel it, use pincers for its extraction.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the easiest thing to remove, which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	During the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat it as we have said in the section and how to deal with discharge, the treatment is not effective, so you must examine the ear in sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If no worm opens, if you treat them with fine tweezers, and they do not open, take the cane from which this form is,
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it should be tight from below and wide from above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert the most subtle instrument into the ear according to the amount of suffering of the patient, then suck on the cane until it forms a complete seal.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Make sure often until all the veins are open.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey to come out, then pinch the cotton around the vein as I have said before.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not protrude as we have said, then administer distills that the ancients have tested in the extraction of worms, and you will find them discussed in the treatment of distills.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and distill your oils and medications into the ear with all these instruments, in this way as you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And whether it is of silver or gold, make thin plates from small openings to distill.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to press for distillation using a well-made silver instrument, and if you see, take a razor and wrap it around the tip with cotton.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever you see of your medicines in the pan, and the fire should be in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then put the razor into the cotton and press with your hand firmly until the oil is distilled or comes out of the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and it makes the patient feel deep pain, and so the distilings appear as if they are burning in the fire, just as they distill into the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and ensure it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	ear inflammation
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born with any perforation in their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and the same thing happens to adults due to a sudden wound or a foreign object in the ear, and this obstruction never completely blocks the ear if it cannot be seen.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and never let the wound become infected, and see that it heals well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	When it happens that the wound does not heal properly, if one cannot see it, it requires different treatments, and in this case, where one can see, it is necessary to place the patient's ear towards the sun.
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the inflammation clearly, and the work has all these symptoms, then this is how it looks:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And make incisions and cuts all around and behind, so that the ear is not damaged.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the operation is on the cartilage or edge of the ear, use fine tweezers and gently pull, while ensuring that all the cartilage is completely cut through.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the inflammations are completely in the ear, take a fine, sharp razor and heat it slightly over the fire, then insert it into the ear canal.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you sense that the patient experiences great pain during the operation, gently perforate and be careful not to damage the edges of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then place a plug according to the width of the perforation and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Make no movement as long as the wound is fresh, or take a cloth and dampen it in rosewater, and sprinkle vitriol powder on it.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swollen, it is necessary that you take the cloth and use another moistened cloth in cerate made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling is gone.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as long as it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, dip a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and use other remedies to remove the bleeding which are treated through distillation.
de la char des papieres	on the subject of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	Consider that when hairs come out in papers from the skin when moist and then dry, it is necessary that you extend them with tweezers and pliers, and cut off the tip with a spatula from its roots.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then place the cold glass on the inflamed joint.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if, after removing the skin, you cauterize with a delicate lenticular cautery, and the healer after incision moves it;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and often they heal, but nothing stays in its place;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized with fire, their roots are burned and do not grow back.
de la gresle	of frost
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times come to paper one thing that seems twisted in its form and hardness, and for this reason, this disease is called "frost," and it is a gathering of great moisture on the paper from above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	The work is as follows:
