pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	take care that the frost is silent on both sides, and this is a slight thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	make the cut deep, then scrape gently from each part, then take it with pincers and cut.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot cover it without piercing the paper a little, it will not harm the patient.
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the fracture is large, with an open wound, treat it until it heals.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, make no great effort, for the inflammations will soon restore it and cause harm.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the pain descends into the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper against it, and use tweezers to pull out the pain, cutting and pressing from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is removed by incision, it causes no harm.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the frost is broken, leave the oil of salt water, and heal the wound of those who have been afflicted until they are well.
de la graisse des eulz	from the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Gripes are a fat that is caused by threads on paper above it, and this happens more often in children than adults, causing them great pain, and they experience catarrh in the mornings, and cannot bear the light of the sun because tears flow to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	and for this reason, they lie on their faces again, and sleep with their eyes closed, and their eyelids are moist from the tears that fill them up, which change their appearance due to the pain that opens in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the joint with your fingers and feel the pain between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of the operation is that the patient places their head on the healthy side.
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take the linen cloth, and prepare a tent in a circular manner according to the amount of discharge from each part, and place it over them.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press your hands on both sides so that the bones come together in line with the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then making a groove in the middle of the moisture with a sharp knife, not wider than the wound made in a vein.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and stitching the skin perfectly until you reach the bones;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and from the groove, pulling with various arrangements, according to the shape of a white fat piece.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Take then from this a whole piece of cloth, dipped in fire, between your fingers and move your hand to the right and to the left until it is dispersed.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and ensure that you do not plug the gap, that you reach all of the grime up to the oil, and do not blow on it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the gap does not open at the beginning, gently widen the gap a little bit.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	then remove it as we have said, then moisten cloth with oil and water, apply to the joint, and stretch in all directions.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such people who grind and apply something to corrupt the moisture that is lingering.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him as long as he is sane.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the hot abscess, treat it with external applications as long as he is sane.
des poilz des papieres	hairs of paper
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When on paper grow hairs that are arranged differently from nature, they become inflamed, causing just as much harm as if they were stones, and bring about types of illnesses such as tears, softening of the papers, and albugine, as long as it is due to the destruction of the hairs.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment is according to four manners:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	or by cautery with fire, or by remedy according to what is present, or in the chapter of cautery; it is done either by incision and stitching, or by binding, according as I shall say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary that you place the patient's head in your healthy hand, then turn the paper from the oil to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it turns out, that is good.
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if it does not turn out, then if he pushes an needle through all the threads above.
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and be sure to cut the edge of the paper where the hairs grow, and pull the thread from above all the way through the paper, and turn it towards the razor.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then making a cut in the skin, adjusting the hairs, smoothing them out completely, from the large tear to the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	then pull out the thread and place under the paper a small piece of cotton and cloth, then sign on the paper a figure of a cross, like the shape of a yew branch, and nonetheless it is important that the figure be according to the quantity that you see the paper rise, which is measured in all.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if at this part, one skilled in the craft uses a great quantity of paper according to how soft the paper is.
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then make incisions throughout all the spatium on both lines that you have marked, starting with a large tear down to a small one.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and it should have one of the splits near the natural hairs thick as a root, then bend the knife in one of the two angles towards the heart, and then peel it completely.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then join the two lips with a stitch using a fine needle and thread, wipe away the blood, and allow the excess tissue to drain from the two edges, without any sticky substances, if you are able to do this.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if this does not help, then leave the stitch and threads for three or four days.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without stitches using dry and constricting things, because the paper will be relieved at the healing of the wound and the gathering of it, but the stitch is moved (as the ancients said), and these are painful tasks.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and it is that you sign the paper with a figure that is like the seal of myrrh, as we have said, at three points, according to the shape that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then take hold of what overcomes the small forces equally according to the form that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the pincers, and the task is not even, take a needle where there is thread, and tie it around the shape.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and tie the other thread through the larger tear, and the second thread through the smaller one, and gather the threads equally between your fingers.
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then gently apply equal pressure with your hand, to the entire skin where you have marked it, as we have said, then gather the two edges of the wound together with stitches, and treat it until it is healed.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess forms at your incision, it can be soothed with wax and similar remedies.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and no time passes when the paper fibers are changed.
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	it is necessary that you use what we have said about incisions;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but sewing in one direction and another is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of fractures is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you convert the paper and make it inside according to what I said, and then make two strings by art, and also fine liens as long as the paper and as wide as the spatula.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut as much as the parts where you hold the strings;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then carefully join both together above what is over the paper of oil, and pull the two strings from the two parts formed.
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it thus for no days, and the skin that is pulled will die and wither and fall off as long as it adheres to him.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it is delayed, if the wound reaches a certain force, then treat it as long as it is healthy.
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and if the wound is infected and pus forms, and when it becomes raised and the paper-like skin does not allow the hair to grow.
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the shape of the two lines you will make according to this figure, and according to this length and width.
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	the work involves piercing with a fine needle, and threading soft and delicate silk thread.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then join the pieces together gently, one to the other, so that the length of the bones is a palm's length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then order in the wound another thin thread of silk briefly, and tie the ends securely with the thread.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then place the patient's head in a healthy position.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and make sure the wound is free from dirt so that the work can be revealed, for it is a delicate and small task, then insert the needle into the entire wound at its root where the hair is attached, and slowly pierce the paper-thin skin until you reach the natural hair beneath.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then extract the hair all the way up to the root, and push the hair back into the root if there are one or two or three or more of them.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then extend your hand until the hairs come out completely from the root in the paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the root is treated and the hairs do not come out with it, then pull the root completely from the inside along the line that you have ordered, until the root comes out fully and you see it through your eye's vision.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	So then, if you remove the wound and the thread, and close it with oil and leave it for two or three days, until the hair returns to its place and the scar heals.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	and if the hairs are small, then accompany them with long natural hair, and either raise it with the one you leave, as long as it is elongated, and then gently lift it.
de la porriture de l’oil	Of the putrefaction of the wound
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this illness called "aleacrati" or putrefaction occurs in the oil, it has two manners:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One is natural, and the other is unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it occurs suddenly from wounds, or cutting, or cautery, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of performing this in the case that you split open the wound, separate the lips of it, and place linen inside, binding it as long as it remains healthy;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and it is not advisable that you use in the treatment of it things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but I work with softening substances, such as fenum (fenugreek).
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the rosewater of water or flaxseed is cooked, and the diaquiled onions melted in any of the oils, it envelops a bandage, and applies it to this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the true treasure of your cure is that you must be careful, so that it does not harden according to its former shape.
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these works that we have spoken are not only remedies for this illness, but to prevent it from returning according to its former form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the grease that comes from oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This illness which is dislocation, truly called "fracture," is both natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident arises from wounds, cuts, cauterization, and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the path of the procedure is such that if you press an needle, it has a double thread, and thread it into the wound, and pierce from the left tear (eye) towards the right, so that the thread comes out in two parts of the wound.
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then the wound is covered with everything, with the needle above, and the pad has a wide spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	and if the shape of the paper returns according to what is necessary, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If this is not done, take a razor and place it in the crevice, turn the paper, and make two cuts on either side within the paper.
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the cuts of the two slits be at the two angles of the incision that you have made, and make them at an angle so that when they are assembled, the shape is like the shape of a letter 'G'.
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove the one that is according to the thickness of its sides from the paper, then adjust the two parts carefully and sew them with a thread of flax.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply the treatment for what we have mentioned about softening and warming medicines, as long as he is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a wound or stitching or cauterization, then you must make a clean slit beneath the skin and paper-like hairs, according to what is mentioned before.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then separate between the two parts of a tent, as I have said before;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and one must perform the work according to the form of the illness, for it is much diverse in form, and skilled masters have devised all sorts of devices to bring back the appearance to its natural state;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patient himself, according to what is necessary for the work and the use of various instruments in many arrangements.
dou soudement de la papiere	The phrase "dou soudement de la papiere" does not have a clear meaning in
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this suture is performed by unskilled hands in such a way that the paper (bandage) on top is smooth with oil and cannot move or perform its natural functions, it is then necessary for you to insert the tip of a razor under the paper and lift it slightly from above.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and stretch it with pincers, as you remove what is hard in the delicate spatula, neither too sharp nor too blunt, so that the patient does not suffer from the spatula being too sharp and cutting through the oil.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and so your incision, from which you have peeled away the assembled part, should be gentle, so that the skin returns to its natural form.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and it heals completely, without ever mixing with foul oil, but rather with clear water and collars.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the skin and oil a thin cloth of linen, and above the oil lay a moistened wool in abundance.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day, use warm collars and suds until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	from the nail of the finger
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	You know that the nail is according to two manners:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	it is nervous and seems hard and dry, and another that is not nervous at all, but seems like white, frozen moisture, which, when touched with iron and treated with pincers, cannot be done by anyone.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both of them begin to extend towards the great tear duct, growing smaller and smaller until they cover the entire vision and all the light and motion of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incision is that the patient places his head on a healthy side, then opens his eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and take the paper in your hand, then curl the finger like small pliers, and stretch it above.
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put a horse's, or deer's, or cow's hair in it, and tie a strong thread.
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the point of the needle slightly and insert it into the finger, and pierce through the entire length of the needle, and tie the finger with thread, extending it above, and scrape all the hair around the side of the nail, immediately after pruning the cuticle and the silk of the hair up to the head, then carefully cut off the remainder at the root with a delicate scalpel or small forceps, leaving the natural shape of the nail intact, so that through the incision no tears come to the habitually sensitive skin.
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and never stretch the fingers at the joint solely, and with thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then the skin is scraped off the entire soft part, which takes the shape of:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	and be sure that the soft part does not touch the flesh and tear it, and that the knife is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, pour a little bit of broth into the wound, and then apply a collar made of litargire (a type of metal) and leave it until the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then focus on the treatment of it until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	If the nail is not firmly attached and you cannot push the needle through, or the hooks cannot enter, this condition of the nail often requires treatment with various medications.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the dissection, and if you see it covered, open gently for the sick person, and take a light spatula according to this form.
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And gently remove the nail from above, and if you see that it shrinks slightly and the pain intensifies, mix a drop of collar (an ancient term for a medicinal substance) made from lightning stone and red string, and apply the oil to the affected area until the next day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then begin the other task according to this same work, as long as it is entirely healed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing in the oil contradicts you, such as a hot abscess, then apply it and treat the hot abscess first until it is healed, and then continue the work as before until it is completely cured.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh causes pain in the eye due to great damage, suspend it at the corner and cut off a part, not all of it, so that no more tears flow.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then distill into the eye a red collar made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	on the flesh that is born on the eyelid
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some men's eyes never turn red, they cover the pupil and rest on papers, twisting them in the fire, and look like a ball of rosin.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	and the work consists of the patient placing their head on a healthy surface, then opening them up, and applying all the appropriate hooks, and supporting it with strength.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	then take the first hook, and go on applying them one by one until the end, taking care not to hurt yourself during the work.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	and let the incision be smooth and delicate, as we have said in cutting a fingernail and with small movements, thus removing the nail as the shape demonstrates after this chapter.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	and when the incision is completed and all the charcoal is removed, apply to it the oil of crushed silk or distil a red collar and similar corrosive medicines, and cover with hot cotton soaked in oil so that it is assuredly hot.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if it does not improve and the pain intensifies, and you doubt that the abscess is hot, leave the oil and treat the abscess with calming remedies for a hot abscess.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	then return to your work as long as it is healthy, and thus make similar cuts adjusted in the oil by this appearance.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	But nevertheless, it is necessary that you pay attention to each weak joint in the natural way;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the unnatural way, in the work of doing;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not put your hand into any of these works as long as you see that this member is suffering from that work.
des voines des eulz	veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	These are the red veins that are covered over the eye, they obscure the sight of their work and weaken the eye every day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	The first task is to look at which joint is affected, for it is severe and out of place, and there is no other disease outside of the joint.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Then instruct him in this manner:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to place his head in a healthy position, then suspend the veins at every point according to his wisdom, and let the veins be fine and double according to this form.
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And there should be two incisions by degrees in the body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then gently compress the veins, and drain the blood hour after hour, until you see the veins disappear from the skin.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to puncture the skin with the forceps, and perform this task at noon in front of the sun, and be very diligent in your work so that you only succeed in draining the veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	and when you have done this, slowly drip the green and red collyrium into the oil to dissolve what is lingering in the wound.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	If you cannot gather all of these at that hour, make a poultice over the oil with soothing things for the pain of the eyes, and leave it for no days until the pain is relieved and the inflammation of the hot eye is assured, then continue in this manner as before until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of strength:
de la fistule de l’oil	From the fistula of the oil
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	They call these "arrested" fistules:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	As you treat it by cautery and medicine for the burning pain as I have previously mentioned, if it does not heal, there is an infection in the abscess where he must die, and remove all moisture from it until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed and you see the corruption and blackness, take all the instruments mentioned here and shape them accordingly.
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called the "sharp point", and it should be made of iron from the base to the tip, and pointed like a lime as it is in the current shape.
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the surface of the corrupted bone, then twist it between your fingers, and press with your hand as much as you know that corruption is gone.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this again, then return to the use of drying medications.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the joints are fused and it grows, and the bowels' wall is fused and remains that way for 40 days, and it does not renew or become abscessed, and no bad accidents come, know that it is healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If there is no other remedy but to bring the fistula back to the opening of the cold according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and it is that you discover the bone a second time by iron or medicine, and when it is discovered, take the foresight according to this form, and let the instrument have three angles, and make the cut reach up to the top as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	then place it on the delicate bone, remove your hand from the oil, and return to the entire instrument until it pierces the bone and the patient feels the pain because if he keeps his hand on his cold,
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	and then restore the joint with dry medicines, as I have taught you, and when the pain subsides and the joints harden, then consider the matter anew.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter matter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	from the wound
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes are fully open and there is no disturbance or pain, it is necessary to keep the patient still.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then apply heat, then use suction cups or a hot compress without causing injury, then apply the oil made of mullein, aloe, incense, and dragon's blood, and then strain the oil, and wrap it with bands and cloth.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the method of bands: if you bind bands soft enough, doubling them in three (or four), and then placing one over the other according to their respective needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then stretch from above with a firm band, and restart the poultices to suck without causing harm;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the poultices and leave the compression for day and night, and if it becomes too tight, it is good to gently stretch it;
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the compression after day and night, and if you see the skin repairing itself, that is good;
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	if the splint, bandages, and bindings, and the leeches are reapplied while he is healthy.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	breakage of the woven fabric
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruptions occur in the wound covering, it opens up and fills with small pieces like grains of resin, and it is encouraging to see.
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it covered, the work is such that you push a needle into the base of the lower part, then another needle where there is a double thread in the upper part.
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and pierce it, leaving the first needle according to the arrangement;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the skin with a double-threaded needle and tie one part of the edge around it, tightening well, then extract the needle and apply the other moist lint in abundance.
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the thread disintegrates with the edge, then treat the wound with comforting things until it heals.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and never should the wound be restrained by any part of a circular bandage until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the joint appears to be well-formed, pierce it with a delicate needle that comes from oil, draw out the white moisture and lower the joint, and it will enter again immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract it as long as it is healthy.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the bow of the oil
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called "alcunnati" is only from moisture that is gathered in the oil, resembling clear water flowing down, but it is not clear water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the manner of the work is that you place the patient on a seat with their legs raised and straight, then take the head in both hands from two sides, and move it until you see the moisture rising towards your fingers.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then it is fixed, and the bandage does not descend or become loose, and the patient can see clearly as before.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not come loose, know that it is urgent, and if the bowel descends, it must be treated as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	if you delay the patient in your hands, then take a fine spatula and make incisions on the corny tissue through the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corny tissue and the cornea, while the bowel is still there.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it comes out, it should be distilled in hot honey or mixed with honey, or boiled water and honey, then treated with another remedy until it is clean.
des aigues de l’oil	The phrase "des aigues de l’oil" translates directly to "of the waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have seen the signs of water in the division, and what is needed to pierce them.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if it is opened according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You should place the patient between your hands crossed, away from direct sunlight, and tie the healthy oil tightly to them.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the paper from oil in your left hand if the joints are on the left, or in your right hand if the joints are on the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then, in your right hand if the joints are on the left, take the instrument called "almagda," or in your left hand if the joints are on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	then, with the tip of the instrument, cut through the crown carefully along the thinnest part near the meatus, then twist the instrument called "almagda" vigorously and move your hand as it pierces into the meatus, feeling that the "almagda" reaches the empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the length of the magical way be exactly the same as the measure of the space from the base to the end of the shadow.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of the oil;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	if you will see the bone on this paper for the clarity of the cornea, then place the instrument exactly there where the water is, and press it from one way to another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If he lowers it now, he will see the patient before him and the instrument in his hand.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting, let the water take the second way, place force with the instrument, and when it is fully inserted and does not rise, slowly extract the magical oil by turning your hand a little at a time.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then put back in acute a little bit of silk string, and remove from these the oil inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then apply heat to the affected oil with hot wax or any other moist oily substance, and wrap it in clean oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, place a hot poultice on it with plenty of fire.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the foreign body cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, as there are some people whose eyelids are too tight, it is necessary that you press the instrument called 'alberit', which has this form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce only the outer joint, and do not go too deep, but make it subtle, then apply almagda, as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and upon completion of the work, prepare for the patient a comfortable place to sleep, so that he sleeps on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and be careful of all movements, and feed him with light foods, and do not move his head to the right or left, and bind him according to his condition for three days.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then dislocate it in the same dark place, test its sight, and make it see nothing, and then put a bandage on it for seven days.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and it is not appropriate that you do this during treatment or after incision now, but it is necessary to lighten it, because the acute pain has increased.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	if an abscess forms after seven days, dislocate it on the seventh day and apply the remedies for a soothing abscess.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is calmed, he should open his eyes and place a side on his face to cover the light, and be in that dark house again.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	and then he leaves the house little by little and returns to his own affairs.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and he should know that no disciple should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And then came to us one from Iran who told us that in their peaceful lands they had a method of perceiving things unseen, from which they drew water, but I have never seen anyone like this in our land, nor have I ever read about it in the books of the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and by chance, this is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the shapes of alchemy, so that those who do not know them will see them.
et soient d’arain proprement:	and let them be of pure gold:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And the center of this same subtlety should be in the middle, and the three corners sharp.
de la char sor le neis	Of the pain near the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	No creature is born or grows with diverse joints, so that there is none that resembles a scorpion in its multitude of limbs.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and if it has such a creature, enriched with beautiful fur, and if its flesh is of a good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In this case where the pain is severe and not chronic, it is necessary that you make the patient lie between your hands facing the sun.
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open the patient's nostrils, and pour the liquid into those that are blocked, and treat them vigorously.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then hold what you can support with the delicate spatula from one side, as long as you know that this blockage is completely opened.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything that cannot be covered, open it with all the delicate and light instruments until nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and without letting your mind wander, if an abscess forms, cut it as necessary;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if these are malignant abscesses, act quickly and cauterize them until the pus is drained and all the debris is removed, then apply fresh, clean, and warm compresses or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the abscess opens and moisture reaches the palate, knowing that it is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if the moisture does not drain as necessary, knowing that there is debris in the bone above, preventing the instruments from cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Then it is necessary that you insert a thread somewhat thick into it, and be careful with your hands, and leave between each a little space as needed.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and place the patient's tooth with the thread in its socket as much as possible, and pull gently until it comes out through the gum.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and often children are taught this way, and it is a light task for him who wishes to do so.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the head that comes through the gum in one hand, and the other head that comes through the mouth in the other hand, and pull one after the other as we who are holding thread do.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do as you know, that the new wound is corrupted, then treat the child, wipe off the blood, and moisten the wound with Egyptian ointment, and put it back on the body as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointment corrodes all that is remaining of the wound.
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then put a bandage on the wound for no more than days until it is healed, and if it needs further treatment with dry medications, then use them.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, from which they distill oils and medications:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	and it should be of silver or gold, resembling an open lamp, like a candle, and lead it accordingly;
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you make a closed candle, it becomes an instrument full of medications to purge the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have many parts on the head to hold it when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	Of the pain near the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a sickness appears in the head near the eyes, called "tul" (or possibly "ulcer"), it grows and becomes great, as long as it is a visible thing to behold.
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	and for this reason, it is necessary that you catch it at the beginning, remove all the bone, and then apply fire or hot medicine to the joint.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if it is delayed in being treated until it becomes great, be careful if it is hard, of pale color, and lacks sensation.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	if he does not let the wound touch any iron because it is an inflamed abscess, for when one treats it, great harm comes to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if the abscess is of a soft consistency, not hard like an arrowhead, and you can easily open it, draining the patient without harm, then treat the wound with dry and cooling things to heal it.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the nose is cut and sewed
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when the continuance of a bone breaks into one of these powerful cartilages, it profits little, for no man.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	One should therefore watch that this does not happen to anyone, if you consider whether the wound is fresh and full of blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then adjust the two lips to one stitch, and treat it until it is healed;
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the lips are dislocated on both sides, it is necessary to cauterize all parts of their healing place until they heal, then adjust the two lips to one stitch and tighten it, and apply powdered dragon's blood and incense dust.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and place a piece of strong glue or other adhesive binding on the powders and leave it until it dries, then treat the wound with medicine until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The method of stitching is such that you join the parts together:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	using needles, as we said in the stitching of the belly;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or with thread, as I have made known to you.
des apostemes des levres	abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	At home, there occurs within the lips an abscess hard as grains of corn, both smaller and larger.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	then you must turn the lips and make an incision on each one, taking them with pincers and cutting into each part.
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	then use the lever after the incision of vitriole powder, until the wound is stained;
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then the lever from silk, and dry the wound with clean things until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	from the work of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times it occurs on the gums, tightly stuck together, which the old call "albulus";
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	so it is necessary that you hold it with pliers and cut at its root, leaving the bow or the vein to flow.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	then place a hot compress on the affected area, or other powders that restrain and desiccate;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	and if the wound returns after incision, and this happens many times, if the cautery is performed a second time,
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return after the cautery;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of the instruments for cauterizing.
des sordens	from disorders
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Never should they be assembled at the base of the teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, or on the rough, unpleasant scales.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	and never are the teeth black and yellow and rotten, as long as the corruption comes to the gums, and they stink.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	it is necessary that you hold the patient in your hands, and their teeth or gums be in your possession, and pull out any visible roots, as long as nothing remains.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and do the same for black, green, yellow, and other hues, as long as they are infected.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if that which is at the first reason is removed, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	If this does not work, start again from the second day and the third, as long as you have everything under control.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and know that teeth require various tools to extract, as the operation shows, because the pliers used to pull out teeth have different shapes from those used to space them.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these shapes and others should be with you, prepared.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When treating a tooth that is causing pain, take your time to gently extract it as much as you can, for no one should do otherwise.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	For it is a very powerful substance, so there is no excuse for cutting it off.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Then, when the patient is in great pain, it is important that you be certain about which tooth is painful.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the patient feels great pain, and thinks it is from a tooth infection, and extracts the painful tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	But the pain does not leave them despite this, as long as the evil tooth is extracted, for we have seen this happen to these saints.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	and when you are certain of the painful tooth, it is necessary that you cut around the tooth with a very sharp knife to protect the gums from all sides.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	then move your fingers or use the fine tweezers on the first slight movement, as long as they are well dislocated, then firmly hold the tweezers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and place the patient's dislocated joint gently between your knees, holding it firmly so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the tooth correctly without breaking it, if it doesn't come out, take none of these instruments and push them gently from every side, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the bone is broken and pierced, it is necessary to fill the space with cloth, either in the wound or the opening.
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if it is squeezed gently with tweezers, so that it does not break when squeezed.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	And one must speak very clearly around the gum to dislodge the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	Be very careful so as not to break it, and if a part breaks off, return the remaining piece to the patient, for due to the evil of the root, he will experience greater pain than before.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And be wary that you do not act like the ignorant healers who, in their haste and foolishness, break the treatment at every turn and do not follow what we have described.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but they bring about this great disease because of the roots that they do not address, or because of the treatment that they break, just as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the tooth is loose, wash the place with wine or vinegar and salt.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and it causes bleeding, which often occurs, if one uses the place of vitriol ground;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the instruments, with which one should first mute the teeth, should be long and blunt, not doubling when pulling the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	and these are the shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And let the members be of good size so they do not bend when pulled, and well-forged of iron, and toothed for proper movement.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains stuck, it is necessary to place a moistened cotton ball with butter on it for one or two days, until the joint loosens, then use pliers called "algefri" to carefully extract it, making the patient feel relieved.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and they should also be made like a file, and this is their shape:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to emerge from these clutches, it is necessary that you uncover the skin all around the root, and place the instrument called "althali", which is a pliers, in this way:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And it should be firm and thick so that it does not break, and if the root jumps out on its own, that is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	if no, even with all the tools, the shapes come as follows:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one uses this instrument with two prongs, the shape is as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools that are used in the reason of teeth, and this instrument that seems like great pliers, whose shape is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let this instrument be strong so it cannot break, and know that many instruments of iron are.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments, which are not mentioned.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and the most skilled surgeons create their own instruments, according to what their works and the illnesses they encounter demonstrate, for there are many diseases that the ancients did not teach about due to the diversity of symptoms; if one breaks a bone or another part, and it becomes stuck, or if it cannot be moved, then if he seeks the appropriate instruments I have mentioned, and uses gestures as an aid, this is how the process goes.
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And they should be thick and well gripped to hold the bone, so that it does not escape but can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	and then return to the patient the appropriate medicine for this, and if there is putrefaction in the bone, small or large, use all these instruments.
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears not according to the natural shape of the body, and its form is ugly, especially in young women, it is necessary that you know if the tooth has grown after the original one, and is not in its proper place, and cannot be filed or smoothed.
adonques lou raie;	then cut it;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if it is caught with a tooth, take this instrument whose shape is like a small beak, and let it be made of hard steel.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the surgeon should hold the tooth firmly in his hands day after day for its hardness, and because you do not move the others, and if it is apparent that it can be filed, then file it from one side as the shape requires.
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	it is also like the lime from which they make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and in the lime, press the tooth gently with your fingers, so that it does not move until it falls out on its own.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then the surface at the end is entirely smooth, and if the cut is too deep it damages the tongue; therefore, it is necessary to file the sharpness until it is even so that it does not damage the tongue or corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the tooth aches.
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the teeth are loose due to biting or pulling, and the patients cannot bite down on anything without pain, they take restrictive medications but that does not help.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if they need to restrict it with a golden thread, for the silver thread turns green and decays, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and so the son's hair should neither be too thick nor too thin, according to the quantity of space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you need to direct the teeth, take the thread and wrap it twice between the two healthy teeth, then place the fragments between the loose teeth, as many as there are, until you reach precisely the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	then restart the covering up to the point where you tied it, and gently but firmly pull your hand, until it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and let your ligature be at the root of the tooth so it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the pieces of thread with pliers, assemble them, and insert them between the healthy tooth and the one with the abscess, so as not to damage the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and then leave it so tight as it can stay, and if it loosens, the threads will pull out, if released from another thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it stays tight for a long time, it will serve thus throughout all its time, and this is the form of the teeth and the alignment of the two healthy teeth, and the two molars, as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth is dislocated, put it back into its place, freshening it as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and do not allow anyone who is not skilled and patient to intervene; and never should the shape of a tooth made from a bone of a deer be used, but rather place it in its missing position and hold it tight as we have said, and wait and serve thus for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	To cut off the language's loose ends.
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Never should these ties that come from beneath the tongue or nature be considered, for thus we are born.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	because of an accidental deep wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the work involves opening the mouth of the patient with pain, placing his head in your hands, and extracting his tongue.
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then cut the thick nervous ligament, as much as the tongue is dislocated from its place, and if there is stiffness or resistance, and it suddenly opens a wound, then draw the hook and cut through that ligament.
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and be careful that the cut does not go too deep, to avoid damaging the artery beneath.
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have done that, lift up the limb with hot water and oil, or cold water, then place a thin strip of linen under the tongue.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and each night, the patient suffers from a condition that prevents their limbs from healing.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if the infection from blood comes, then put a hot compress on the limb made from crushed vitriol.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	and if the pain from the infection goes away, then cauterize it with a hot iron, which is good for healing.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then treat with another remedy as long as he is healed,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see it is of any red, black, or hard color, so that the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is cancer.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	and if it turns to white and there is moisture, cut the tumor with a fine blade, and remove it from both sides.
