vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	then empty it, taking half or a third, for if you remove more than is necessary at that moment, the patient may die due to the dissipation of their spirit from the weapon, or they may lose consciousness, or they may draw close to death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but according to the amount of its virtue, and according to what the disposition of the virtue in the sick person signifies, and its pulse.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then take the instrument and hold the water, and it is now held by the force that stops the opening above the sinus, of which I have spoken, so that you pierce according to this manner.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then resume the instrument the next day, if you see the patient suffering, and take a small quantity of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	Take no action, and guard against any sudden movements as long as it does not cause any pain but a little water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and leave too much water, treat the wound with dry soil or hot sand, and use sweat or a bath and sunlight, and color it with wine.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat with drying medicines as long as it is healthy, and cauterize the stomach and liver and spleen after draining the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	from the obstruction of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	No child is born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it is necessary at any time for him not to pierce through all the very subtle particles according to this form.
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then make or find a subtle hole in the bladder, and close it and hold it thus for three days or four, and when he wants to urinate, open the closure, let him urinate, then close it again.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and if by chance he doesn't remember, because the strong flow of urine does not allow the closure to be kept closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	If the closure is small, it is a sign of a weak bladder, as we have said, and it will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have a hole in their bladder are blighted, because no one is born with a hole at the top of the penis, so they cannot urinate until they close their penis.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot move because the material cannot reach the joint, and this is a bad illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of the operation is that the patient lies on their back, then the head of the bone and the neck are extended as if they were a quill, so that the opening to the middle is created as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be careful of the discharge of blood which comes many times, and if it happens, apply pressure to stop the bleeding, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	from the pimples of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times this illness comes to the tree (limb), and it appears as a ugly deformity;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and it has malignant and benign forms;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	you must then press them gently, and wash and clean them all, then place moist cotton in an Egyptian dressing;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continue the treatment with the dressing until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the affliction is malignant, with a putrid and foul appearance, it requires cautery treatment.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have achieved it, and if the splint is in a state of rest on the bone, with part of it inside the skin and part outside, then it is necessary to remove the splint that is inside first.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and if it is sewn shut, then open it.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	Because when you bind it together, unless the pieces of the bone are perfectly aligned, it will cause discoloration and corruption in the bone and limb.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	so it is necessary to remove all black and corrupt parts, then apply a paste made of honey and flour from red apple bark and leaves, and continue to treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if a blood clot comes, then instruct the lunar cauterizer according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterization helps if it follows the combined dispositions:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, at the discharge of pus, and at the corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the tip of the rod is corrupted and withdrawn, it is necessary that you drive or guide a stick into the pus and drain the patient;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the hair is dried at the tip of the rod that has happened to those who have not been circumcised, or it becomes a wound or an abscess, it is then necessary that you scrape it with a sharp instrument, until the cords are loosened and the part from the rod is freed;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if it is a difficult thing to devise, then you should cut it with a sharp instrument at the base of the stick and the blade.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then separate the pieces gently, and place a thin cloth soaked in cold water between them, so they do not stick together again.
de la circoncision	On circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a complete healing process like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	however, when we perform this operation of our own will, and especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best and most gentle work for their health.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcising their children, for they do not practice it in their laws, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have observed most of the masters and elders who performed circumcision near the anus, and how they use force, and all sorts of new tools.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	if the threads were to break because there are two of them, and by chance one is cut above and the other below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	or he might cover it again, and the pain becomes doubled, and the purification, which should be near the anus, is not assured for the point of the member.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and to the purification of the nail, if by chance the fire escapes and runs away, the work will be ruined, and often times they grow like this, needing no purification, which I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleansing that is done with force on all the fibrous threads, I have found the benefit of experience, for the forces cut exactly as well from above as from below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, if it is cut evenly throughout, then you release all tension.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but ensure the thread is well wrapped around the skin.
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and be sure of the method in the first attempt so that if the child hears you and understands that you are only tightly winding the thread around the stick, then afterward, make it relax in all ways as much as possible.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then stretch it straight between your hands and restore the strength in your hands or beneath your feet so that the demon does not see any of these.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then take your hand to the staff and blow through your nostrils, holding it up until the end of the staff is covered.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then cleanse it well of the dirt that is gathered on it, then tie the limb with a double thread, and bind it to another bandage.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it at the second joint with your two fingers and thumb, and cut between the two bands, then gently lift the end of the staff.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow drop by drop, for it is the cause of pain.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on it and on the powder I apply a glue made from egg whites cooked in rose water, mixed with oil of roses, good and fresh, and leave it until the next day, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The way to purify the body is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Both feet should be clean and cut, and the toes also, as equal as possible to the rest:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error in purification is when the veins inside bleed during the incision:
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Then you must extend your finger, so that the joint creates an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and hold it even, and if you cannot hold your finger, with pincers if you have them, then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they remain for three days, and the skin beneath the arrow is swollen, leave it until the abscess heals, and gently peel away the scabs.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	if the abscess heals as well as you can see, and it protects the part of the arrow, it will not harm anything.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Cure therefore the place suddenly wounded by powder, which we have spoken of treating in the section on powders, and if one takes too much heart, and it goes above, then it will not harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure it therefore, as we have said, while it is healthy.
dou retenement de l’urine	retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is an indication of a stone or frozen blood, or bowels or a chronic illness, or similar conditions, as we have spoken of in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine cannot be released, and you see a retention due to a stone in the bladder or neck of the bladder, then it is necessary that the patient bend over on their knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place them incorrectly on the back, extending their belly from above the back and restraining the patient in any way possible.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then they constrict the collar of the bladder to the position of the stone above, causing the urine to flow freely.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should administer an extraction with all the instruments called "syringes", which have this form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and let them be fine, light silvered hairs, like the feathers of a bird.
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and the blade should be one palm length and a half, and fine at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method for urination is that you take a double thread, tie it around the base with a wool or cotton ball, and then insert the thread into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut off the excess thread, then insert it all into the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit down, and drain the bladder using moist oil and olive oil and lukewarm water.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the shaft, until it reaches the base of the shaft, then bend the shaft upwards towards the opening.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then squeeze the syringe before reaching the bladder, and feel the patient's pain until it reaches the empty space, and this is not done according to these orders because the direction in which it is guided is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then gently pull the thread through the wool little by little, and the urine follows the thread, then extract it firmly, and stop the flow of urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and begin the syringing as soon as the bladder is empty, and arrange the patient comfortably.
des maladies de la vessie	Of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scabs or pus comes to the bladder, where putrefaction is assembled, you should view it distill water and medicines, by using the entire instrument called 'clepsydra', and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and if it opens again:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	from one side, and from the other, as you can see.
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the hair roots, by which the compresses cut well the wound without added harm, if we can drain the moisture and press as much as necessary.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicines moving in the bladder, place the keen-edged knife into the moisture, and pull gently until it comes out.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	if you pull out the moisture with the knife, then quickly twist the limb firmly again;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	if the moisture goes deep inside, reaching the bladder now, so that the patient feels it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of a gentle enema, whereby the bladder is enemaized;
si est ci:	If there is a burn:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is of silver or gold, and the joint is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and takes it out from within the chest where the joint is attached;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture you intend to use for a warm bath, then wrap it between the two breasts, forming a good double-layered seal, and heat the moisture over fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the catheter into the urethra and press your hand against the bladder to expel all the moisture until the patient feels that the bladder is empty.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, and make a circle of it, and punch it through with a round hole.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread into these openings, and reassemble the circle as if you were closing it, and put inside what you see of oil and moisture and water, and secure it with the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do the same as you did with the bladder, pressing it with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	from the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already discussed the methods of stone and arrow extraction, along with various medications.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and we have also spoken of the distinction between stones that cause pain and all their signs, and in what type of stone one must perform surgery.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that stones in the bladder occur more often in children, and this is a sign of acute urinary retention, similar to water in its subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and open the wound wide, and greatly ease the patient of their pain, and probe many times, and then it heals;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and at the mouth of these sores, we destroy their foundations;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is gentle until they are four years old, and it is much more difficult for the elderly, and it is halfway between for those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the treatment is lighter for those who have great stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with a enema, in order to expel all feces from the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it often gets stuck when trying to pass a stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and straighten them, and move them from side to side, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and never moves up again.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit between your hands with his legs apart, so that the bladder is tilted downward.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then take the stone and touch it inside.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not give way to the touch at all, dampen your index finger with oil from your left hand, and if the patient is old, or your middle finger with oil from your right hand, and if the patient is young and fully grown;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and press it into its base, and hold the stone, and when you feel it in your hand, if there is an infection at the base of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press with your finger, and the stone will come out from where you see it cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the physician to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to extend the testicles with his right hand, and with his left hand remove the skin that covers them in the area where the incision is made.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then he extracts the spatule, which gives it this form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an opening between the testicles and the base, not in the middle but on the side of the left thigh.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and it should be straight on the stone, and your fingers close together or at the base, and make the cut across so that it is wide enough to accommodate the stone, but narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	In case the pressure becomes so great that it has to leave its place, allowing it to depart without effort.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and knows that there is a hard part where it has corners or edges.
si est griés a issir;	if it is caught trying to escape.
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if it is in a part that is smooth, resembling a ball, and round, with a light opening.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	At such points where it has corners and edges, make the size larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not fall, you must use pliers that are like a file on the head to extract the stone so that it does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	you then use a small, curved instrument on the head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot do it this way, if the hole is wide, and the stone is large, then extract it with a strong pull like vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there are multiple stones, first extract the largest one from the bladder's neck, then cut it out, and afterward, pull out the smaller ones if there are any others.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, you must cut it out carefully, and make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For there are two things that happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	or he dies, or the urination returns immediately, as the muscles cannot contract.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless, make every effort to gently pull or remove debris with tweezers, as long as you treat it piece by piece.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, compress it, and place a moist cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then resolve the patient's pain on their collarbone, and do not loosen the bandage for three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you dislocate it, if a lot of hot and cold oil and water arises, then apply curative ointment and basic ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses form in the wound and cause corrosion, and blood clots in the bladder, and due to this the urine is retained, which is known in this manner as without warning with the urine.
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	so press your finger on the wound, and extract the blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder, and rot.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then open the wound with fire and hot oil, and draw out any debris, and aid it in every way you can, as long as it is clean.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that all the hours you treat him, you bind both thighs to him, and gather the medications on the joint.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, it is caught in the urethra, and stuck in place, and the urine cannot pass through.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if you treat it as I say, cutting many times, then the size of the cut is an excuse for the size due to this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this myself.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take the first piece of iron according to this form and insert it at three angles into one tisson.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the urethra beyond the stone, so that it cannot go back into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then gently twist the drill in the wood until it reaches the stone.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the drill back to your hand in the stone little by little, as you can drill through the stone from another side.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	if urine comes, then press your hand against the part that is stuck inside the wood.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	if it is broken and bursts with the urine, and the patient is in pain;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason, then pull the stone out from inside and another from above, then make the stick go around the stone between the two bones, then extract it strongly, and loosen the ligament, and clean the frozen blood in the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it while it is healthy.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones" (a reference to kidney stones)
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It is rare for stones to occur in women, and if they do, the treatment is difficult, and it is hindered by three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin.
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second reason is that it is difficult to find a woman who is well-versed and reveals herself to men, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way is that, by chance, one cannot find a woman well-versed in this art of healing.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth way is that the stone in women's bodies is often harder than in men, so it requires deeper incision and much fear. If this situation arises, you should seek a knowledgeable midwife, and if you cannot find one, do not hesitate to use this subtle knowledge on a chaste woman.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and it presents a wise dance in the life of women, where a woman who knows a part of the art, and instructs her to do what you command regarding the examination of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully observe if this woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must remove her hand or finger and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, by stretching her hand down her finger, and restraining it from moving, she should instruct the patient to remove their finger or hand with the pain, and press and squeeze their left hand on the swollen bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If it is cut, it is necessary to move it slowly and gradually from the entrance of the bladder down to the thigh root.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then cut into the stone at the thigh root, near the middle of the hard mass, where it is most mobile and feels the pain in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move the stone from above or below, but make the first cut small.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the saw into the cut, feeling the stone so deeply in the wound that it can come out fully, and know that there are many ways of cutting stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	This is to know, small and large and sharp and smooth, long and round, and which have roots.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	knowing these similarities to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the wound does not heal, mix vinegar and apply it to the place, and keep it for an hour until the pain is relieved.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your task, as long as the stone is hard, and have the tools I told you for removing stones from people to help you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the wound persists, and it is an artery that has been cut, apply powder to the place and press with bandages and bends, and do not repeat this, leave the stone and do not extract it again, unless the patient dies.
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed and the swelling goes down, then return to your work while the stone is still firm.
de hernie carnouse	herniated cartilage
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ripe water is nothing other than the assembly of moisture or white mucus, which is detached from the heart of things, containing the fire.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "syfac" and never properly in the web of fire, if one believes that it is another fire.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin around the thing between the white mucus that we have spoken of;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this happens no more.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this rice is due to weakness in the skin, which causes it to spread and accumulate matter.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And it never happens from striking the testicles, and this moisture takes many forms.
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it changes to jaundice, or has no red, or black, or clear white, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition, for if it is as white as we have said, then the abscesses are red, very long, like a snake's figure, and do not open the testicles, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the affected skin, the abscesses are red with a part of the flesh, and for that reason one thinks it is another flesh.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white part, one should feel it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you see to know the color of the moisture, try to pull out all the intrusive matter, from which the form is as it is above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what follows, judge of what is inside after the introduction.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we cure it with iron, the patient must be healed according to their strength and the replenishment of their body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lie down on your back, on one thing a little high, and place under him several sheets of cloth.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on your left side, and instruct the helper to sit on your right, and stretch the rod towards one of the two ribs at the heart's edge.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the scalpel, and cut through the skin of the ribs from top to bottom, making a slit entirely straight by dividing the rib cage tissue until it turns white, and carefully remove it according to each rib's power.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the swollen part with a sharp tool into a wide opening, and extract all the fluid, then place your fingers, and the swelling will subside.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the center of the swelling, but only the affected area.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all or in pieces along its side carefully, for if you do not cut it cleanly and sharply, the fluid will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the air bubble rises to your work, then return it to its place when you have completed the work with the swelling.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then gather the two books of the heart's edges together with a stitch, and treat it as other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the heart corrupted by another illness, then it is necessary that you bind the vessels that are suspended, in doubt of the flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	then cut the edge at all the suspension, and extract the heart, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the vein is gathered into two parts together, knowing that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you treat the other part just as you did the first, then wipe off the blood, and apply a fresh, moistened lint cloth with rose oil to the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and apply another moistened cloth with wine and oil, and place two cushions on it, and cover them with doubled cloths, and bind it to all parts according to this form.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, make them of shredded wool according to this shape and join them together by sewing in the groin of the breeches, one at the front leg root up to the back, and the other at the hand joint.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two joints on both sides of the shoulder, gathering all the restrictions in the loop of the collarbone;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and never apply this cautery with a red-hot iron, but rather use a delicate surgical knife to make the incision, and cut through the flesh of the joints, and keep it warm as we have said before, so that the white part containing the blood is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if you take the cautery according to this form, and pierce this white part in small incisions, and then apply this hot cautery gently:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And the doctor, in every way you can, as long as you stretch everything out.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and ensure that the fire does not touch the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and be careful about the decay of pus, and monitor for signs of infection from the work of great size;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything goes against you, whether it's an abscess or pus discharge or any other issue, treat what contradicts you, according to what has been said before.

dou chastrement	Dou chastrement (Double cautery)
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Knowing that castration is forbidden in our law, and for this reason, I would prefer not to speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is not necessary for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one is that it should answer honestly when asked, and know the treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate some animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say, therefore, that castration is performed according to two manners:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction, or by division.

et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and do this for a long time, and apply a dry linen tent to it.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then he shall be cured of other ailments as long as he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is swelling from heat, if it is not an abscessed wound, it needs to be treated in this way:
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an abscessed swelling in the heat, it should not be probed or punctured.
des emorroides	Of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that, without usual care, become enlarged and when hemorrhoids have been present for a long time, they thus become involved.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have previously described in the division the similarities and signs, and I will now say those that receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and their complications, when they are in the advanced stage during pregnancy, are not easily detected, unless they require treatment with heat.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the opening of the vagina can be felt; these are those that can be treated.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is therefore necessary that you place the woman in a cold house, then stretch the other as pliers, and squeeze it at its roots, then apply powders of medicinal herbs to stop the blood, such as witch hazel and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then he immerses his feet in the wall for an hour, then places them in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if the fever persists, one should apply a poultice of sumac and bark from pomegranates and gall nuts and similar things, and then take flour from barley, mix it with honey and lard, and make an ointment to apply on his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is still wet, that's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If this does not help, apply suction cups on the back without injuring the nipples;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take linen, and soak it in juice of plantain or in juice of olive with old wine, and place it on the joint.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has subsided, continue the treatment with the wound as long as it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles a sharp point, so it should be covered as I have said in the previous text.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then continue the treatment until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	about abscesses of the breast
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses occur in the body, such as cancer and previous abscesses, and sores and ulcers and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is therefore necessary that I tell in this treatise the hot abscess which comes in the margin, which is not at all an abscess that draws bow-shaped.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know the work of iron, look if the abscesses are active at the beginning of their appearance, and are full of heat and fever, and if they turn red, then you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hasten to pierce, but let it die as long as the pain is calmed;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then make the patient lie down, and have him take a few small positions where he bends, supports himself on his back, and brings his feet closer to the affected leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and spread his thighs apart, and place his arms below his knees, and bind them tightly with a strong band.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then turn the patient towards the right side, and bring the instrument used to open the wound, which afterward forms the shape.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you bring the instrument to perform this procedure, you first insert the tip to determine the depth of the wound, so that when you insert the instrument afterward, it does not go further than required, and does not harm the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with fine cloth, so that the instrument does not hurt.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he places the cone of the instrument above and shades the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and it is done gently with the hand, it is necessary to cover the head and guide the spatula.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowel is empty, it is necessary that you place in the wound moist tents soaked in rose oil or dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the clean tent over the wound directly on the breast, and put over the wound and the lying hand a moist cloth dipped in water or mullein;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound after two days of healing have passed, as long as it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and never raise the wound and the breast with a enema of water and honey, and then water or cooked roots of lily and long aristology.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the wound dressing.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is healed in the ulcer, it is necessary to avoid heating with iron, but treat it as we have said in the preceding section.
de l’enfantement	from childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	Trade is most important in birth than she knows the shape of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman struggling down, and desires to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child should be hastened to be born.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then know that these children are according to the natural shape, and their heads come first, followed by the rest of their bodies.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press the belly, so that the child is born quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	because when it descends towards its head, it accompanies him, and it empties the marrow of its excesses through good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this, which comes otherwise, does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it never comes upon its feet, but rather pierces the body or limb, or comes up onto the belly, or back, and turns by chance upon its neck, or takes other malicious forms;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	so it is necessary to be skilled in movement so that it is wise and subtle in these matters, casting aside error and disappointment, and I will show you all the forms of how one should assist it.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the fever comes upon the head through natural causes, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, making her rest on a saddle, or as women hold it;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and if its nature is of oil or fennel, cooked, then take a small spatula in the shape of which we have spoken and apply it between his teeth.
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the second layer, cutting with his fingernail as deep as the moisture that is embedded within.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's belly as the child descends, and if it does not descend, it is necessary to enemas the woman with fennel mucilage mixed with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make him sneeze and cough from a cold condition, and hold his mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if now the child is born.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands rise up, it is necessary that you gently reset them little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, place the woman on her side, and raise her feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then stand him up on the ground, and tie the woman so she does not try to stand;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if his hands cannot enter, and the child dies, if he cuts them with a knife placed before him, and extracts the child, then reset them equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	From the exit of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto its feet, it is necessary to push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it slightly and slightly until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then press from the feet and extend little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	He can jump as high as his feet allow, if he is commanded to press, and the act makes him sneeze due to the condition.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if he jumps, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not happen as we have said, if it is turned little by little, according to its natural form.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it becomes slightly easier.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come as we have said, take some moss from a high place, and oil of hawthorn, and melted resin, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and place it on the nature of the woman inside and outside this treatment, then make her lie in hot water up to beneath the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened, she should be given a collar of myrrh, placed upon her, and left for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her lie upon a seat, then have her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose closed, and gently press on her stomach, for the baby is now ready to be born.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from the emergence of the child onto its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the baby is in this position, he will gently move his hands little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then it must be rested on his collarbone, with the weight hanging down, and he lies on his side.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	he bends his hands little by little and then grabs the patient's belly, removing the cushions from below until it is completely relaxed.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if it is not successful, he takes hold of the feet and moves them, then moves the belly up, and finally pulls with his hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and gently pulls the child.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to press until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the birth of the child who comes out with a large hand during
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I wish to learn how to bring back the hand.
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be brought back, then raise the woman and let her go.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot go, then lay her on the bed and straighten her legs.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then apply the musk as I have described.

de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the birth of the child on its mother's chest, with its hands spread and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I know that the pain takes hold of her hand, then she squeezes it little by little and gently.

et la fai esternuer.	and make it sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same manner, throughout all of this.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes about in this manner at regular intervals, if the moisture is removed with your finger, as long as it empties.

adonques si istra legierement.	then gently pull it.
de l’issue des gemelz	from the opening of the eyes
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that many times twins are born, and never three or four.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an unusual thing, and it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and they do not live long, being called thus.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply, and are devoured by the pleasure which creates them, which is connected to the bow.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and they never leave as naturally as all of us, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they become serious, if the cure is as we have said, and there are subtle symptoms, making them too sudden and light in their effect.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do it so that it is moved towards health.
de plusors enfans	from many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	No joints are formed in the human body as in I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more than XV, and they are all shaped like a child according to the measure of his noble wisdom, and it is necessary for the skilled surgeon to know all this, for perhaps something similar may happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	it is done according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you cure a woman with a dead child in her womb, as I have said in the previous section, and it will not come out, and you are forced to use manual force;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	If it is necessary for you to know if the woman is of sound mind and does not fear death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be lying on her back, and her legs inclined downwards.

et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he holds the twist in his right hand, and places the curve between his fingers of his left hand, and stretches it slightly with all his hand, and inserts the twist into any of these joints we have said, as long as it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the bone:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then find another bone, where the third one is missing, so that the extraction is even.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it equally from one side to the other, to pull out, and let the bones bite so that they hold, just like this shape:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if part of it remains stuck, take neither oil nor any tool to it, but press the other part and pull;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if it persists, lower this incise or raise it higher, and do until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes forward before the other and cannot return due to tightness, it is necessary that you wrap it with a cloth until it releases completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then cut at the joint of the foot or the knee, and it is necessary that you do the same with the other hand, and hold both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the baby's head is large and stuck in the birth canal, or it has a sharp, bent assembly, it is necessary that you press the spiny forceps between your fingers, and do so until the head emerges and extract the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	You use the instrument called an "almidach" to shape it with the tools and chapter that follow this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus, I myself make it attach naturally at a great cost.

Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	and if it is twisted in the stomach or the bowels, you must extract it at the drape (or fold) wrapped around the hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and making the stomach or bowels empty, until the moisture inside is drained;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if any other parts are broken and the feces remain, then press the hand into the wound from the anus, and pull it towards the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then I press the bone deeply, and pull it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the opening of the wound has narrowed due to hot abscess that formed, it is not advisable to work on it at all, but instead one should apply moist and greasy things.

Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the limb is on its side, and you can make it even, apply what we have said for the living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if he cannot move it, even if it is cut into pieces, he should not leave any of the secondine behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when this is done, he should be given what we have said about the incisions in the abscesses that come near the mare.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if the bleeding from the abscess comes, it should be treated with immediate restraint, and other remedies should be administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose stomach had been cut, and another doctor had treated it, and prevented further harm.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, a swelling appears in the cheek, it swells up so much that it opens, and it begins to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called upon for treatment, and I thought for a long time, but I could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong poultice, and an egg came out, and after a few days, others followed.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed because that belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	If I thought this was a bone from a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I examine the wound, and pull out the bones as much as possible, until the woman is in better condition.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and examine the woman long tens thus, and then withdraw a little bow from its place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not recorded this chapter for any other reason than that, when the master encounters a strange thing, he knows how to provide aid.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the woman back to her place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	After this comes the form of pressure, with which one binds the books.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at the second turn, as the second joint of the limbs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more subtle in their tightening, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth should be wide enough to fit two fingers' width and the edge of the tree trunk, about one palm and a half long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and also adjust both limbs to the same tension of this same horn, firmly joined together, about half a palm's length or slightly more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and this dual adjustment is screwed into the mouth of the horn to open it when you turn both horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, resembling tweezers.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it should have two adjustments, as you see, of one palm length, and two fingers width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the vagina opening fully to the instrument, have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread and her knees bent, then carefully adjust the two adjustments together in the vagina, and hold the end of the instrument from below between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then use your hand to handle all the instruments, just as you did with the pliers evenly, according to the amount that you see open the mouth of the wound, until the pain ceases to do what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	all these instruments are skillfully crafted, and there are many of their kinds, each resembling the other;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when you see them properly equipped, the work is done more quickly, and with greater ease for the practitioner due to their quality.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not disregard the instrument even if you have not arranged it, for the necessity does not excuse the lack of preparation.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second stage of labor is reached, it is important that you instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze gently, while holding her hands at the mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she jumps from there, that's fine.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If the bone does not come out, I will take a sharp tool or an opening, and insert herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, such as calament, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all of these herbs, or none of them, should be cooked or boiled in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then insert a cane or an opening into the pot, and put the other end in the mouth of the wound, and hold it until the vapor goes inside the wound;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make him sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the treatment does not help, then proceed with the next step.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if after this treatment she remains weak, and is not strong, she is instructed to wet her left hand with oil of sesame or musk, then wrap it in a cloth and leave it in that state, and seek the second treatment.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, she should press and stretch it little by little straight, so that the marble does not break during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it is necessary to move slightly to the right and left, and then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	if it comes and goes.
